  <script type="text/javascript">
   $(document).ready(function(){
	//정부기관명으로 찾기 탭 클릭
	$(document).on('click','div#government_pop > ul.layerPop_tab > li > a',function(){		
		$('div#government_pop > ul.layerPop_tab > li > a').removeClass("selected");
		$(this).addClass("selected");

		var govIndex = $('div#government_pop > ul.layerPop_tab > li > a').index($(this));

		$('div#government_pop div.layerPop_tab_contents').hide();
		$('div#government_pop div.layerPop_tab_contents').eq(govIndex).show();
	});

	//다국어입력기
	$('div.detail_btnBox > p.worldwordBtn a').click(function() {
		$('.worldwordBox').show();
		$(".worldword .language a.selected").focus();
		//다국어 입력기 위치이동
	});
	//다국어입력기 이동
	$(".worldwordBox").draggable();

	//상세검색창 닫기
	$('.detailSearchBox a.close').click(function() {

		$('.layerPop_box02').hide();
		if ( $(this).parents(".detailSearchBox").hasClass("pop01") ){
			$(".img_detail_search").focus();
		}else {
			$(".img_detail_search2").focus();
			}

	});


	//엔터 이벤트 생성
	$("form[name=detailSearchForm] input[type=text]").on('keydown',function(e){
		if(e.keyCode == 13){
			goDetailSearch();
		}
	});
});


//정부간행물 조직도 클릭
function ReturnDataCommonTwo(data1, data2)
{
	$('input[name=guCode8]').val(data1);
	$('input[name=gu8]').val(data2);
	
	$('.layerPop_box .bg').click();
}
//레이어팝업
function layer_open(elemendId,obj){
	
	
	
	//자료이용하는곳 이미지 경로 변경
	if(elemendId == "placeMapView"){
		var placeMapSrc = $(obj).attr("place-map-src");
		var placeArtText = $(obj).text();
		$("div#placeMapView div.layer_photoBox > img").attr('src',placeMapSrc);
		$("div#placeMapView div.layer_photoBox > img").attr('alt',placeArtText);
	}	

	//별치기호
	$('#taste_pop').html("");
	if(elemendId == "taste_pop"){
		aptSearch();
	}

	//한국대학명
	$('#college_pop').html("");
	if(elemendId == "college_pop"){
		UniSearch();
	}

	//한국정부기관명
	$('#government_pop').html("");
	if(elemendId == "government_pop"){
		GovSearch();
	}

	//분류기호참조
	$('#kdc_pop').html("");
	if(elemendId == "kdc_pop"){
		SearchKDCFrame('1');
	}
	
	//한고목 기관명
	$('#korcisLib_pop').html("");
	if(elemendId == "korcisLib_pop"){
		libSearch();
	}
	

	var $target = $('#' + elemendId);		//레이어의 id jquery 객체
	var $bg = $("div.layerPop_box div.bg"); //레이어 background

	$(".layerPop_box").show();
	$("div.layerPop").hide();
	$target.show();

	// 화면의 중앙에 레이어를 띄운다.
	if ($target.outerHeight() < $(document).height() ) {
		$target.css('margin-top', '-'+$target.outerHeight()/2+'px');
	}else{
		 $target.css('top', '0px');
	}
	
	if ($target.outerWidth() < $(document).width() ) {
		$target.css('margin-left', '-'+$target.outerWidth()/2+'px');
	}else{
		$target.css('left', '0px');
	}

	//레이어의 닫기 버튼을 눌렀을 때
	$(document).on('click','a.layerPop_close',function(e){
		$('.layerPop_box').fadeOut();
		e.preventDefault();
	});

	//레이어의 배경을 눌렀을 때
	$('.layerPop_box .bg').click(function(e){
		$('.layerPop_box').fadeOut();
		e.preventDefault();
	});
	
	
}		


// 판종
function change_the(input_name)
{
	if ($("#context_type").val() != "")
	{
		$.ajax({
			type: "GET",
			async: true,
			dataType: "html",
			url:  "/nl/search/SearchDetailForm.nl?searchmode=DetailForm009Action&edit_class=" + $("#context_type").val() + "&input_name=" + input_name,
			data: "",
			error: function(){
				//alert('error');
			},
			success: function(msg){
				$("#edit").html(msg);
			}
		});
	}
}

//도서관검색
function libSearch(){

	var kwd = $("#keyword").val();

	dataValue = ({"field":"","service":"KORCIS", "form_name":"detailSearchForm", "input_name":"lib"
		, "searchmode":"DetailForm008Action","keyword":kwd});
	
	$.ajax({
		type: "POST",
		data:dataValue,
		async: false,
		//dataType: "html",
		url:  "/nl/search/SearchDetailForm.nl",
		error: function(){
			alert('error');
		},
		success: function(msg){
			$('#korcisLib_pop').html(msg);
		}
	});

}


//별치기호 검색
function aptSearch(){

	var kwd = $("#keyword").val();

	dataValue = ({"field":"", "form_name":"detailSearchForm", "input_name":"guCode3"
		, "searchmode":"DetailForm002Action","keyword":kwd});
	
	$.ajax({
		type: "POST",
		data:dataValue,
		async: false,
		//dataType: "html",
		url:  "/nl/search/SearchDetailForm.nl",
		error: function(){
			alert('error');
		},
		success: function(msg){
			$('#taste_pop').html(msg);
		}
	});
}

//한국대학명 검색
function UniSearch()
{
	var kwd = $("#keyword").val();

	dataValue = ({"field":"", "form_name":"detailSearchForm", "input_name":"guCode7", "input_name2":"gu7"
		, "searchmode":"DetailForm003Action","keyword":kwd});
	
	$.ajax({
		type: "POST",
		data:dataValue,
		async: false,
		//dataType: "html",
		url:  "/nl/search/SearchDetailForm.nl",
		error: function(){
			alert('error');
		},
		success: function(msg){
			$('#college_pop').html(msg);
		}
	});

}

// 한국정부기관명
function GovSearch()
{
	var kwd = $("#keyword").val();

	dataValue = ({"field":"", "form_name":"detailSearchForm", "input_name":"guCode8", "input_name2":"gu8"
		, "searchmode":"DetailForm004Action","keyword":kwd});
	
	$.ajax({
		type: "POST",
		data:dataValue,
		async: false,
		//dataType: "html",
		url:  "/nl/search/SearchDetailForm.nl",
		error: function(){
			alert('error');
		},
		success: function(msg){
			$('#government_pop').html(msg);
			
			if(kwd != undefined && kwd != ""){
				$('div#government_pop > ul.layerPop_tab > li > a').eq(1).click();
			}
		}
	});
}

function SearchKDCFrame(pageNum){

	$("div.layerPop_cont").off();//스크롤 이벤트 제거
	var kwd = "";
	if($("#keyword").val() != undefined) kwd = $("#keyword").val();
	var field = $("form[name=detailSearchForm] select[name=gu2]").val();

	dataValue = ({"field":field, "form_name":"detailSearchForm", "input_name":"guCode2", "searchmode":"DetailForm001Action","keyword":kwd,"int_Index":pageNum});
	
	var tempHtml = "";
	tempHtml += "<div class=\"layerPop_top bgType02\">";
	tempHtml += "    <h1>분류기호명 찾기<\/h1>";
	tempHtml += "    <span class=\"close\"><a class=\"layerPop_close\" href=\"#\"><img src=\"/nl/_res/img/bg/bg_layerpopup_layerPop_top_close.png\" alt=\"닫기\"><\/a><\/span>";
	tempHtml += "<\/div>";
	tempHtml += "<!-- layerPop_tit -->";
	tempHtml += "<div class=\"layerPop_cont_srch\">";
	tempHtml += "    <dl>";
	tempHtml += "        <dt>분류기호명<\/dt>";
	tempHtml += "        <dd>";
	tempHtml += "            <input name='keyword' id=\"keyword\" value=\""+kwd+"\" type=\"text\" class=\"input_txt\" title=\"분류기호 입력\" onkeydown=\"if(event.keyCode==13){SearchKDCFrame('1');}\">";
	tempHtml += "            <a class=\"btn_bk\" href=\"#none\" OnClick=\"SearchKDCFrame('1');\">검색<\/a>";
	tempHtml += "        <\/dd>";
	tempHtml += "    <\/dl>";
	tempHtml += "<\/div>";
	tempHtml += "<!-- layerPop_cont -->";
	tempHtml += "<div class=\"layerPop_cont type02\" style=\"height:350px;\">";
	tempHtml += "    <table class=\"tblStyle02\" summary=\"분류기호,분류기호명\">";
	tempHtml += "    <caption class=\"hide\">분류기호 목록<\/caption>";
	tempHtml += "    <colgroup>";
	tempHtml += "        <col width=\"120\"><col>";
	tempHtml += "    <\/colgroup>";
	tempHtml += "    <thead>";
	tempHtml += "        <tr>";
	tempHtml += "            <th scope=\"col\">분류기호<\/th>";
	tempHtml += "            <th scope=\"col\">분류기호명<\/th>";
	tempHtml += "        <\/tr>";
	tempHtml += "    <\/thead>";
	tempHtml += "    <tbody id=\"kdc_pop_list\">";
	tempHtml += "<tr>";
	tempHtml += "<td colspan=\"2\"><\/td>";
	tempHtml += "<\/tr>";
	tempHtml += "    <\/tbody>";
	tempHtml += "    <\/table>";
	tempHtml += "<\/div>";
	tempHtml += "<!-- //layerPop_cont -->";
	tempHtml += "<div class=\"layerPop_bonBox\">";
	tempHtml += "    <ul>";
	tempHtml += "        <li><a class=\"layerPop_close\" href=\"#\">닫기<\/a><\/li>";
	tempHtml += "    <\/ul>";
	tempHtml += "<\/div>";
	if(Number(pageNum) == 1) $('#kdc_pop').html(tempHtml);
	
	$.ajax({
		type: "POST",
		data:dataValue,
		async: false,
		//dataType: "html",
		url:  "/nl/search/SearchDetailForm.nl",
		error: function(){
			alert('error');
		},
		success: function(msg){
			
			if(Number(pageNum) == 1){
				$('#kdc_pop_list').html(msg);			
			}else{
				$('#kdc_pop_list').append(msg);
			}
			
		},
		complete : function(data) {
            // 통신이 실패했어도 완료가 되었을 때 이 함수를 타게 된다.
		if(Number(pageNum) == 1) $("div.layerPop_cont").scrollTop(0);
		$("div.layerPop_cont").scroll( function() {//스크롤이벤트 생성
			  var elem = $("div.layerPop_cont");
			  if ( elem[0].scrollHeight - elem.scrollTop() == elem.outerHeight())
			    {				      					  
			       SearchKDCFrame(Number(pageNum)+1);
			    }
			});
            // TODO
      	}
	});
}



// 공통 결과 선택 이벤트 (코드+이름)
function ReturnDataCommon(data1, data2, inputName1, inputName2)
{
	var form_name = "detailSearchForm";

	if(inputName1 != ""){
		document.forms[form_name].elements[inputName1].value = data1;
	}
	
	if(inputName2 != ""){
		document.forms[form_name].elements[inputName2].value = data2;
	}

	//close
	$('.layerPop_box').fadeOut();
	e.preventDefault();
}


function goEdit(getUrl, v){
	var hf = document.forms["historyForm"];
	//var frm = $("form[name=historyForm]").serialize();//POST
	//var re_frm = frm.replace(/%/g,'%25');//POST
	$.ajax({
		type: "GET",
		async: true,
		dataType: "html",
		url:  getUrl+"?q="+v.value,
		//data: "re_frm",
		error: function(){
		//alert('error');
	},
		success: function(msg){
			$("#gu10 option").remove();
			var arrList = msg.split("|");

			$("#gu10").append("<option value=''>적용안함</option>");
			for(var i=0; i< arrList.length; i++){
				var arrData = arrList[i].split(":");
				$("#gu10").append("<option value='"+arrData[0].replace(/\s/g,"")+"'>"+arrData[1]+"</option>");
			}
		}
	});
}

	if (navigator.deviceName == "iPhoneWeb" || navigator.deviceName == "androidWeb" || navigator.deviceName == "iPad") {

	function popupOpen2(mypage, myname, w, h, scroll, option) {
		//document.domain = "nl.go.kr";  ////

		var LeftPosition = (screen.width) ? (screen.width-w)/2 : 0;
		var TopPosition = (screen.height) ? (screen.height-h)/2 : 0;
		var settings = 'height='+h+',width='+w+',top='+TopPosition+',left='+LeftPosition+',scrollbars='+scroll+option;
		window.open(mypage,myname,settings);
		return;
	}

	function popupOpen3(myname, w, h, scroll, option) {
		var LeftPosition = (screen.width) ? (screen.width-w)/2 : 0;
		var TopPosition = (screen.height) ? (screen.height-h)/2 : 0;
		var settings = 'height='+h+',width='+w+',top='+TopPosition+',left='+LeftPosition+',scrollbars='+scroll+option;
		if(confirm('로그인하셔야 이용가능합니다\n로그인하시겠습니까?')){
			loginOpenMy(myname, w, h, scroll, option);
		}
		return;
	}



	function loginOpen(myname, w, h, scroll, option) {
		document.domain = "nl.go.kr";
		var LeftPosition = (screen.width) ? (screen.width-w)/2 : 0;
		var TopPosition = (screen.height) ? (screen.height-h)/2 : 0;
		var settings = 'height='+h+',width='+w+',top='+TopPosition+',left='+LeftPosition+',scrollbars='+scroll+option;
		window.open('',myname,settings);
		$("#ssoLoginForm").attr("target", myname).submit();
		return;
	}

	function loginOpenMy(myname, w, h, scroll, option) {
		document.domain = "nl.go.kr";
		var LeftPosition = (screen.width) ? (screen.width-w)/2 : 0;
		var TopPosition = (screen.height) ? (screen.height-h)/2 : 0;
		var settings = 'height='+h+',width='+w+',top='+TopPosition+',left='+LeftPosition+',scrollbars='+scroll+option;
		window.open('',myname,settings);
		document.ssoLoginForm.returnUrl.value="http://www.nl.go.kr/nl/mypage/data/copy_mail.jsp";
		$("#ssoLoginForm").attr("target", myname).submit();
		return;
	}



	function popupOpen(mypage, myname, w, h, scroll, option) {
		document.domain = "nl.go.kr";
		var LeftPosition = (screen.width) ? (screen.width-w)/2 : 0;
		var TopPosition = (screen.height) ? (screen.height-h)/2 : 0;
		var settings = 'height='+h+',width='+w+',top='+TopPosition+',left='+LeftPosition+',scrollbars='+scroll+option;
		window.open(mypage,myname,settings);
		return;
	}

/*******************************
* [저자별검색] step1
* @param tabName
*******************************/
function goMainAcStep1(tabName){
	var acname = $('#'+tabName+' input[name=acname]').val();
	// 3depth 영역 초기화 추가
	$("#"+tabName+" > div.step3 > div.stepContents").removeClass("active").html("");
	if(acname == ""){
		var msg = "저자명을 입력하세요.";
		if("browsingAuthorTab02" == tabName) msg = "단체명을 입력하세요.";
		alert(msg);
		return false;
	}

	dataValue = ({"acname":acname,"tabName":tabName});

	//var frm = $("form[name=historyForm]").serialize().replace(/%/g,'%25');
	$("#"+tabName+" > div.step2 > div.stepContents").html("<img alt=\"loading\" src=\"\/nl\/_res\/img\/img\/result_loading2.gif\" style=\"margin:80px 0px 0px 80px\" \/>");

	$.ajax({
		type: "GET",
		async: true,
		dataType: "html",
		url:  "/app/nl/search/ajax/main_ac_1depth.jsp",
		data: dataValue,
		error: function(){
			//$("#facetAuBox").hide();
			$("#"+tabName+" > div.step2 > div.stepContents").html("");			
		},
		success: function(msg){
			$("#"+tabName+" > div.step2 > div.stepContents").html(msg);
		}
	});

}

function goAcPage(num,tabName){
	$('#'+tabName+' form[name=acHistoryForm] input[name=pageNum]').val(num);
	$('#'+tabName+' form[name=acHistoryForm] input[name=tabName]').val(tabName);

	var frm = $("#"+tabName+" form[name=acHistoryForm]").serialize().replace(/%/g,'%25');

	//$("#"+tabName+" > div.step2 > div.stepContents").html("<img alt=\"loading\" src=\"/nl/_res/img/img/result_loading2.gif\" style=\"margin:80px 0px 0px 80px\"/>");
	$("#"+tabName+" > div.step2 > div.stepContents").prepend("<img alt=\"loading\" src=\"/nl/_res/img/img/result_loading2.gif\" style=\"margin:80px 0px 120px 80px\"/>");

	$.ajax({
		type: "GET",
		async: true,
		dataType: "html",
		url:  "/app/nl/search/ajax/main_ac_1depth.jsp",
		data: frm,
		error: function(){
			//$("#facetAuBox").hide();
			$("#"+tabName+" > div.step2 > div.stepContents").html("");
			//$("#facetAu").html("<div>데이터 가져오기에 실패하였습니다.<\/div>");			
			
		},
		success: function(msg){
			$("#"+tabName+" > div.step2 > div.stepContents").html(msg);
		}
	});
}


//[저자별검색] step2
function goMainAcStep2(acKey,tabName){
	dataValue = ({"ac_control_no":acKey});

	//var frm = $("form[name=historyForm]").serialize().replace(/%/g,'%25');
	$("#"+tabName+" > div.step3 > div.stepContents").html("<img alt=\"loading\" src=\"/nl/_res/img/img/result_loading2.gif\" style=\"margin:80px 0px 0px 80px\"/>");

	$.ajax({
		type: "GET",
		async: true,
		dataType: "html",
		url:  "/app/nl/search/ajax/main_ac_2depth.jsp",
		data: dataValue,
		error: function(){
			//$("#facetAuBox").hide();
			$("#"+tabName+" > div.step3 > div.stepContents").html("");
			//$("#facetAu").html("<div>데이터 가져오기에 실패하였습니다.<\/div>");			
			
		},
		success: function(msg){
			//$("#"+tabName+" > div.step3 > div.stepContents").html(msg);
			$("#"+tabName+" > div.step3 > div.stepContents").replaceWith(msg);
			/* marc 보기 이벤트 생성*/
			$(document).off('click', '#'+tabName+' > div.step3 > div.stepHead > a.markBtn');
			$(document).on('click','#'+tabName+' > div.step3 > div.stepHead > a.markBtn',function() {
				marcview(acKey);
				return false;
			});
			
		}
	});
}
//[저자별검색] 마크보기
function marcview(ac_control_no){
	var url = "/app/nl/search/ajax/marcview.jsp?ac_control_no="+ac_control_no;
	var win = window.open(url, 'popup_marcview','width=750,height=640,scrollbars=yes,toolbar=no,status=no');
}

function goDetailSearch(cate){
	var f = document.forms["detailSearchForm"];

		if($(this).val() != "") dFlag= true;

		return false;

		f.isbnCode.value = f.isbnCode.value.replace(/\-/g,"");
	}

	 var detailUrl2 = "search_gov.jsp";
	 var detailUrl3 = "search_wonmun.jsp";

	f.submit();
	
}

/********************************************
 * 주제명 검색
 ********************************************/
	function goSubject(){
		var f = document.forms["subjectSearchFormMain"];	
		
		var subjectIdx = $("#subjectSelectdBoxMain div.cont ul.lst li").size();
		
		if(subjectIdx == 0){
			alert('검색어를 입력하세요.');
			return false;
		}else{
			$("#subjectSelectdBoxMain div.cont ul.lst li").each(function(i){				
				var subjectText = $(this).find("strong").text();
				if(i != 0) f.subject.value += "|";
				f.subject.value += subjectText;
										
			});
			f.submit();	
			
		}
	}

/********************************************
 * 주제명을 이용한 검색 왼쪽 목록
 ********************************************/
	function goSubjectLnbListMain(){

		var frm = $("form[name=frm_SubjectThesaurusMain]").serialize().replace(/%/g,'%25');
		
		if($("form#frm_SubjectThesaurusMain > #str_SearchWord").val() == ""){
			alert('주제명을 입력하세요');
			return false;
		}	
		
			
		$.ajax({
			type: "POST",
			async: true,
			dataType: "html",
			url:  "/nl/search/SearchDetailForm.nl",
			data: frm,
			error: function(){
				alert('error');
			},
			success: function(msg){
				$('#subjectLeftListMain').html(msg);
			}
		});
	}
	
	
/********************************************
 * 주제명을 이용한 검색 오른쪽 목록
 ********************************************/
	function GetThesaurusSearch(TermID){
	
		$.ajax({
			type: "GET",
			async: true,
			dataType: "html",
			url:  "/nl/search/SearchDetailForm.nl?searchmode=SubjectThesaurusGetAction&int_TermID="+TermID,
			error: function(){
				alert('error');
			},
			success: function(msg){
				$('#subjectRightListMain').html(msg);
			}
		});
	}
	
	/********************************************
	 * 시소러스 DB에서 확장검색으로 선택했을 경우
	 ********************************************/
	function insertThesaurusWord(str_NamedQuery) {
		
		var text = document.createTextNode(str_NamedQuery);
		var selectLi = document.createElement("li");
		var delImg = document.createElement("img");
		var selectStrong = document.createElement("strong");
		var imgA =	document.createElement("a");
			
		delImg.src="/nl/_res/img/btn/btn_close.png";
		delImg.alt="삭제";		
		
		imgA.appendChild(delImg);
		selectLi.appendChild(selectStrong).appendChild(text);
		selectLi.appendChild(imgA);
		
		// 확장된 쿼리
		$("#subjectSelectdBoxMain div.cont ul.lst").append(selectLi);
		document.forms["subjectSearchFormMain"].subject.value="";//선택할때 subject 초기화
		
	}

	$("#subjectSelectdBoxMain div.cont ul.lst li a").live("click", function(){
		$(this).parent().remove();
	});


	/****************************************
	 * 상세검색 입력값 초기화
	 ****************************************/
	function goDetailClear(){
		$("form[name=detailSearchForm] input[type=text]").val("");
	}

	/*****************************************
	 * 상세검색
	 * 자료구분 선택
	 *****************************************/
	
	/*****************************************
	 * 상세검색
	 * 자료구분 선택
	 *****************************************/
	$("div.classify_data > dl > dd > ul > li input[type=radio]").on("click",function(){
		
		var checkedIndex = $("div.classify_data > dl > dd > ul > li input[type=radio]").index($(this));
		
		$("div.classify_data > dl > dd > ul > li input[type=radio]").removeAttr("checked");
		$("div.classify_depth").hide();
		$(this).attr("checked","checked");
				
		$("#classify_data01Text").text($(this).parent().find("label").text());
		$("#classify_depthText").text("");
		//하위 depth 있는 구분 > 1:단행자료,2:연속자료,3:멀티미디어자료,4:장애인자료,5:웹정보자료
		if(checkedIndex == 1 || checkedIndex == 2 || checkedIndex == 3 || checkedIndex == 4 || checkedIndex == 5){
			$("div#"+$(this).attr("name")+"Depth").show();	
		}	
		
		//하위 구성 초기화
		$("table.tblStyle01 tbody tr").hide();
		var tableObj = $("table.tblStyle01");
		
		$("table.tblStyle01 input").val("");//탭 클릭시 value 값 초기화

		
		if(checkedIndex == 0 || checkedIndex == 1 || checkedIndex == 2 || checkedIndex == 3 || checkedIndex == 4 || checkedIndex == 6 || checkedIndex == 7){
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(0).show();
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(1).show();
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(2).show();
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(3).show();
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(5).show();//표준부호
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(6).show();//분류기호
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(7).show();//청구기호
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(8).show();//한국대학명
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(9).show();//한국정부기관명
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(10).show();//판종유형/판종
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(11).show();//CIP제어번호
			
			tableObj.eq(1).find("tr").eq(0).show();//본문언어
			tableObj.eq(1).find("tr").eq(1).show();//쪽당출력건수
			tableObj.eq(1).find("tr").eq(2).show();//자료형태
			
			//tableObj.eq(2).find("tr").eq(0).show();//자료이용하는 곳
		}else if(checkedIndex == 5 || checkedIndex == 11){//웹정보자료, 국가자료종합목록
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(0).show();
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(1).show();
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(2).show();
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(3).show();			
		}else if( checkedIndex == 8 || checkedIndex == 9){//해외수집기록물, 기타
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(0).show();
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(1).show();
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(2).show();
			//tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(3).show();
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(5).show();
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(6).show();
		}else if(checkedIndex == 10){//출판예정도서
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(0).show();
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(1).show();
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(2).show();
			//tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(3).show();
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(11).show();
		}else if(checkedIndex == 12){//한국고전적종합목록
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(0).show();
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(1).show();
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(2).show();
			//tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(3).show();	
			tableObj.eq(1).find("tr").eq(3).show();///도서관
			tableObj.eq(1).find("tr").eq(4).show();//판종
			tableObj.eq(1).find("tr").eq(5).show();//내용형식
		}
		//select box option 변경
		if(checkedIndex == 1 || checkedIndex == 2 || checkedIndex == 8){//단행 목차 옵션 추가
			//$("select[name=f1]").append("<option value=\"toc_keyword\">목차<\/option>");
			//$("select[name=f2]").append("<option value=\"toc_keyword\">목차<\/option>");
			//$("select[name=f3]").append("<option value=\"toc_keyword\">목차<\/option>");
			//$("select[name=f4]").append("<option value=\"toc_keyword\">목차<\/option>");
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(4).show();//목차
		}else{
			//$("select[name=f1] option:eq(4)").remove();
			//$("select[name=f2] option:eq(4)").remove();
			//$("select[name=f3] option:eq(4)").remove();
			//$("select[name=f4] option:eq(4)").remove();
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(4).hide();//목차
		}

		if(checkedIndex == 2){//연속간행물 ISSN 선택
			$("select[name=isbnOp] option:eq(1)").attr("selected", "selected");
		}else{
			$("select[name=isbnOp] option:eq(0)").attr("selected", "selected");
		}
		setDisabledCheck2($("table.tblStyle01 select[name=f5]").val(),$("table.tblStyle01 input[name=v5]").val());
		
	});

	/*****************************************
	 * 상세검색
	 * 목차초록 검색어 입력 시
	 * @param v1: selectbox value, v2: input value
	 *****************************************/
	function setDisabledCheck(v1,v2){

		if((v1 == "toc_keyword"||v1 == "abs_keyword") && v2.length > 0){
			$('select[name=isbnOp]').attr("disabled",true);
			$('input[name=isbnCode]').attr("disabled",true);
			$('select[name=and6]').attr("disabled",true);

	function setDisabledCheck2(v1,v2){
		var tableObj = $("table.tblStyle01");

		if((v1 == "toc_keyword"||v1 == "abs_keyword") && v2.length > 0){
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(5).hide();//표준부호
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(6).hide();//분류기호
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(7).hide();//청구기호
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(8).hide();//한국대학명
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(9).hide();//한국정부기관명
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(10).hide();//판종유형/판종
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(11).hide();//CIP제어번호			
			tableObj.eq(1).find("tr").eq(0).hide();//본문언어
			tableObj.eq(1).find("tr").eq(1).hide();//쪽당출력건수
			tableObj.eq(1).find("tr").eq(2).hide();//자료형태
		}else{
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(5).show();//표준부호
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(6).show();//분류기호
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(7).show();//청구기호
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(8).show();//한국대학명
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(9).show();//한국정부기관명
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(10).show();//판종유형/판종
			tableObj.eq(0).find("tr").eq(11).show();//CIP제어번호			
			tableObj.eq(1).find("tr").eq(0).show();//본문언어
			tableObj.eq(1).find("tr").eq(1).show();//쪽당출력건수
			tableObj.eq(1).find("tr").eq(2).show();//자료형태
		}
	}

          <script type="text/javascript">
           //자동 완성 사용  예제 - 구축 페이지에 맞게 변경하여 사용하세요
	var urlPage		= "/app/nl/search/common/module/akc.jsp";
	var domainNo	= 0;
	var inputID		= "akcKwd";
	var arrowID		= "akcArrow";
	var canvasID	= "akcBox";
	var akc			= null; //전역으로 사용할 경우가 아니면 ready 함수 내부에 정의해도 됨
	
	//검색함수
	var search = function(keyword, rank, tag, num){		
			goMainSearch(keyword);
	};
	
	var hover = function(keyword, rank, tag, num){
		var node = document.getElementById("test");
		var html = "";
		if(keyword){
			html += "keyword = " + keyword + "<br/>";
		}
		if(rank){
			html += "rank = " + rank + "<br/>";
		}
		if(tag){
			html += "tag = " + tag + "<br/>";
		}
		if(num){
			html += "num = " + num + "<br/>";
		}
		//node.innerHTML = html;
	};
	
	$(document).ready(function(){
		akc	= new KonanAKC();
		akc.setAKCComponentID(inputID, arrowID, canvasID);
		akc.setAKCCanvasPosition({left:0, top:49, width:600});		
		akc.setAKCExtraView(true, true, true);
		akc.setAKCConnectionInfo(urlPage, domainNo);
		akc.init(search, hover, true);
	});
          </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   function setCookie( name, value, expiredays ) { 
	var todayDate = new Date(); 
	todayDate.setDate( todayDate.getDate() + expiredays );   
	document.cookie = name + "=" + escape( value ) + "; path=/; expires=" + todayDate.toGMTString() + ";" 
	
}

$(document).ready(function(e) {
	
	cookiedata = document.cookie; 
	if ( cookiedata.indexOf("popLayer_main=done") < 0 ){
		$("#popLayer").show();
	 } else {
		$("#popLayer").hide();
	 }
	 $("#popCloseBtn").click(function(e) {
		$("#popLayer").hide();
    });
	$("#dChk").click(function(e) {
		setCookie( "popLayer_main", "done" , 1 );
		$("#popLayer").hide();
    });
	/*
	$("#popLayer").hide(); */
});
  </script>
